【1】Service Orchestration in the Computing Continuum: Structural Challenges and Vision
- **标题**: 计算连续体中的服务编排：结构挑战和愿景
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15794
> **作者**: Boris Sedlak,Víctor Casamayor Pujol,Ildefons Magrans de Abril,Praveen Kumar Donta,Adel N. Toosi,Schahram Dustdar
> **摘要**: 计算连续体 (CC) 集成了从边缘到云的不同处理基础设施层，通过无处不在且可靠的计算来优化服务质量。然而，与中央架构相比，异构和动态基础设施增加了服务编排的复杂性。为了指导研究，本文首先总结了 CC 的结构问题，然后设想了跨 CC 的自主服务编排的理想解决方案。作为一个实例，我们展示了主动推理（一种来自神经科学的概念）如何支持自组织服务不断解释其环境以优化服务质量。尽管如此，我们的结论是，现有的解决方案都无法实现我们的愿景，但服务编排的研究面临着一些结构性挑战。最值得注意的是：提供标准化的模拟和评估环境来比较编排机制的性能。这些挑战共同概述了 CC 中弹性且可扩展的服务编排的研究路线图。
> **Abstract**: The Computing Continuum (CC) integrates different layers of processing infrastructure, from Edge to Cloud, to optimize service quality through ubiquitous and reliable computation. Compared to central architectures, however, heterogeneous and dynamic infrastructure increases the complexity for service orchestration. To guide research, this article first summarizes structural problems of the CC, and then, envisions an ideal solution for autonomous service orchestration across the CC. As one instantiation, we show how Active Inference, a concept from neuroscience, can support self-organizing services in continuously interpreting their environment to optimize service quality. Still, we conclude that no existing solution achieves our vision, but that research on service orchestration faces several structural challenges. Most notably: provide standardized simulation and evaluation environments for comparing the performance of orchestration mechanisms. Together, the challenges outline a research roadmap toward resilient and scalable service orchestration in the CC.

【2】Evaluation of Dynamic Vector Bin Packing for Virtual Machine Placement
- **标题**: 虚拟机放置的动态向量装箱评估
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14704
> **作者**: Zong Yu Lee,Xueyan Tang
> **摘要**: 虚拟机放置是云计算中高效利用数据中心物理机资源的关键挑战。虚拟机放置可以表述为 MinUsageTime 动态向量装箱 (DVBP) 问题，旨在最小化物理机的总使用时间。本文评估了非透视、透视和学习增强在线设置中最先进的 MinUsageTime DVBP 算法，其中项目持续时间（虚拟机生命周期）分别是未知、已知和预测的。除了文献中的算法之外，我们还开发了几种新算法或增强功能。使用 Microsoft Azure 的真实数据集进行了实证实验。讨论了实验结果的见解，以探索在实践中运行良好的算法结构和有前景的设计元素。
> **Abstract**: Virtual machine placement is a crucial challenge in cloud computing for efficiently utilizing physical machine resources in data centers. Virtual machine placement can be formulated as a MinUsageTime Dynamic Vector Bin Packing (DVBP) problem, aiming to minimize the total usage time of the physical machines. This paper evaluates state-of-the-art MinUsageTime DVBP algorithms in non-clairvoyant, clairvoyant and learning-augmented online settings, where item durations (virtual machine lifetimes) are unknown, known and predicted, respectively. Besides the algorithms taken from the literature, we also develop several new algorithms or enhancements. Empirical experimentation is carried out with real-world datasets of Microsoft Azure. The insights from the experimental results are discussed to explore the structures of algorithms and promising design elements that work well in practice.

## 数字图书馆(cs.DL:Digital Libraries)

【1】Artificial Intelligence Specialization in the European Union: Underexplored Role of the Periphery at NUTS-3 Level
- **标题**: 欧盟的人工智能专业化：外围国家在 NUTS-3 级别的作用尚未得到充分探索
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15249
> **作者**: Victor Herrero-Solana
> **摘要**: 本研究考察了 2015 年至 2024 年期间 NUTS-3 水平下欧洲地区人工智能 (AI) 研究成果的地理分布。使用来自 Clarivate InCites 的文献计量数据和引文主题分类系统，我们分析了两个层次的主题聚合：电气工程、电子与计算机科学（宏观引文主题 4）和人工智能与机器学习（中观引文主题 4.61）。我们计算了 781 个 NUTS-3 区域的相对专业化指数 (RSI) 和相对引文影响力 (RCI)。虽然巴黎（法兰西岛）、华沙和马德里等主要大都市中心在绝对产量方面处于领先地位，但我们的研究结果表明，外围地区，特别是东欧和西班牙，表现出最高水平的相对人工智能专业化。值得注意的是，我们发现区域专业化和引文影响力之间几乎没有相关性，并确定了四个不同的区域概况：高影响力的专业化区域（例如格拉纳达、哈恩、维尔纽斯）、高影响力但低影响力的区域（例如布加斯、波兰的几个地区）、高影响力的非专业化区域，其中菲因（丹麦）作为一个显着的异常值脱颖而出，尽管专业化程度较低，但仍实现了卓越的引文影响力（RCI > 4），以及多元化的投资组合选择性卓越（例如德国地区）。这些结果表明，人工智能研究为外围地区提供了发展有竞争力的科学领域的战略机遇，尽管要获得国际知名度需要的不仅仅是研究量。
> **Abstract**: This study examines the geographical distribution of Artificial Intelligence (AI) research production across European regions at the NUTS-3 level for the period 2015-2024. Using bibliometric data from Clarivate InCites and the Citation Topics classification system, we analyze two hierarchical levels of thematic aggregation: Electrical Engineering, Electronics & Computer Science (Macro Citation Topic 4) and Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning (Meso Citation Topic 4.61). We calculate the Relative Specialization Index (RSI) and Relative Citation Impact (RCI) for 781 NUTS-3 regions. While major metropolitan hubs such as Paris (IIle-de-France), Warszawa, and Madrid lead in absolute production volume, our findings reveal that peripheral regions, particularly from Eastern Europe and Spain, exhibit the highest levels of relative AI specialization. Notably, we find virtually no correlation between regional specialization and citation impact, identifying four distinct regional profiles: high-impact specialized regions (e.g., Granada, Jaen, Vilniaus), high-volume but low-impact regions (e.g., Bugas, several Polish regions), high-impact non-specialized regions, with Fyn (Denmark) standing out as a remarkable outlier achieving exceptional citation impact (RCI > 4) despite low specialization, and diversified portfolios with selective excellence (e.g., German regions). These results suggest that AI research represents a strategic opportunity for peripheral regions to develop competitive scientific niches, though achieving international visibility requires more than research volume alone.

## 离散数学(cs.DM:Discrete Mathematics)

【1】FO and MSO Model Checking on Temporal Graphs
- **标题**: 时间图上的 FO 和 MSO 模型检查
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14592
> **作者**: Michelle Döring,Jessica Enright,Laura Larios-Jones,George Skretas
> **摘要**: 算法元定理提供了一个重要的工具，用于显示由结构限制定义的图类上的图问题的可处理性。虽然静态图的此类结果已经很好建立，但时间图的相应框架相对有限。在这项工作中，我们回顾了过去逻辑元定理在时间图上的应用，并开发了一个扩展的统一逻辑框架。我们的第一个贡献是引入了参数顶点间隔成员资格（VIM）宽度和树间隔成员资格（TIM）宽度的逻辑编码，这些参数随着时间的推移捕获顶点和组件活动的签名。在此基础上，我们将现有的有界寿命和时间程度的一元二阶 (MSO) 元定理扩展到参数 VIM 和 TIM 宽度，并为所有四个参数建立新的一阶 (FO) 元定理。最后，我们为各种时态图问题标注了可重用 FO 和 MSO 公式的模块化词典，并给出了一个例子。该词典允许组合地表达新问题，并直接在我们考虑的四个参数中产生固定参数的易处理性结果。
> **Abstract**: Algorithmic meta-theorems provide an important tool for showing tractability of graph problems on graph classes defined by structural restrictions. While such results are well established for static graphs, corresponding frameworks for temporal graphs are comparatively limited. In this work, we revisit past applications of logical meta-theorems to temporal graphs and develop an extended unifying logical framework. Our first contribution is the introduction of logical encodings for the parameters vertex-interval-membership (VIM) width and tree-interval-membership (TIM) width, parameters which capture the signature of vertex and component activity over time. Building on this, we extend existing monadic second-order (MSO) meta-theorems for bounded lifetime and temporal degree to the parameters VIM and TIM width, and establish novel first-order (FO) meta-theorems for all four parameters. Finally, we signpost a modular lexicon of reusable FO and MSO formulas for a broad range of temporal graph problems, and give an example. This lexicon allows new problems to be expressed compositionally and directly yields fixed-parameter tractability results across the four parameters we consider.

## 数据结构和算法(cs.DS:Data Structures and Algorithms)

【1】Local Node Differential Privacy
- **标题**: 本地节点差分隐私
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15802
> **作者**: Sofya Raskhodnikova,Adam Smith,Connor Wagaman,Anatoly Zavyalov
> **摘要**: 我们在私有数据分析的本地模型中发起了对图的节点差分隐私的研究。在我们的模型中，称为 LNDP，每个节点都会看到自己的边缘列表，并在此输入上释放本地随机化器的输出。这些输出由不受信任的服务器聚合以获得最终输出。我们为此设置开发了一种新颖的算法框架，使我们能够在输入图度分布的模糊近似上准确回答任意线性查询。对于某些自然问题，生成的算法与中心模型中的节点隐私可实现的准确性相匹配，其中数据由可信服务器保存和处理。我们还证明了 LNDP 所需误差的下限，这意味着我们的算法对于几个基本图统计数据是最优的。然后，我们将这些下限提升到交互式 LNDP 设置，即使在允许不断进行多轮交互的情况下，也证明了我们算法的最优性。获得我们的下限需要新的方法，因为为通常的局部模型开发的方法不适用于图形中固有的重叠输入。最后，我们证明了结构结果，揭示了本地节点隐私与表格数据的标准本地模型之间的质的差异。
> **Abstract**: We initiate an investigation of node differential privacy for graphs in the local model of private data analysis. In our model, dubbed LNDP, each node sees its own edge list and releases the output of a local randomizer on this input. These outputs are aggregated by an untrusted server to obtain a final output. We develop a novel algorithmic framework for this setting that allows us to accurately answer arbitrary linear queries on a blurry approximation of the input graph's degree distribution. For some natural problems, the resulting algorithms match the accuracy achievable with node privacy in the central model, where data are held and processed by a trusted server. We also prove lower bounds on the error required by LNDP that imply the optimality of our algorithms for several fundamental graph statistics. We then lift these lower bounds to the interactive LNDP setting, demonstrating the optimality of our algorithms even when constantly many rounds of interaction are permitted. Obtaining our lower bounds requires new approaches, since those developed for the usual local model do not apply to the inherently overlapping inputs that arise from graphs. Finally, we prove structural results that reveal qualitative differences between local node privacy and the standard local model for tabular data.

【2】A Weighted-to-Unweighted Reduction for Matroid Intersection
- **标题**: 拟阵交集的加权到未加权约简
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15702
> **作者**: Aditi Dudeja,Mara Grilnberger
> **摘要**: 给定同一地面集上的两个拟阵 $\mathcal{M}_1$ 和 $\mathcal{M}_2$，拟阵交集问题是找到最大基数公共独立集。在问题的加权版本中，目标是找到最大权重公共独立集。在各种设置下寻找针对该问题的有效近似算法一直是一个令人感兴趣的问题。在许多模型中，未加权和加权版本的最著名结果之间存在差距。在这项工作中，我们解决了缩小这一差距的问题。我们的主要结果是减少将任何 $α$ 近似未加权拟阵交集算法转换为 $α(1-\varepsilon)$ 近似加权拟阵交集算法，同时通过 $\log W$ 因子增加算法的运行时间，其中 $W$ 是纵横比。我们的框架是多功能的，可以转化为流和单向通信复杂性等设置，其中拟阵交集得到了充分研究。作为我们技术的副产品，我们在这些模型中得出了加权拟阵交集的新结果。
> **Abstract**: Given two matroids $\mathcal{M}_1$ and $\mathcal{M}_2$ over the same ground set, the matroid intersection problem is to find the maximum cardinality common independent set. In the weighted version of the problem, the goal is to find a maximum weight common independent set. It has been a matter of interest to find efficient approximation algorithms for this problem in various settings. In many of these models, there is a gap between the best known results for the unweighted and weighted versions. In this work, we address the question of closing this gap. Our main result is a reduction which converts any $α$-approximate unweighted matroid intersection algorithm into an $α(1-\varepsilon)$-approximate weighted matroid intersection algorithm, while increasing the runtime of the algorithm by a $\log W$ factor, where $W$ is the aspect ratio. Our framework is versatile and translates to settings such as streaming and one-way communication complexity where matroid intersection is well-studied. As a by-product of our techniques, we derive new results for weighted matroid intersection in these models.

【3】Fair Correlation Clustering Meets Graph Parameters
- **标题**: 公平相关聚类满足图参数
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15683
> **作者**: Johannes Blaha,Robert Ganian,Katharina Gillig,Jonathan S. Højlev,Simon Wietheger
> **摘要**: 我们研究了相关聚类的泛化，它通过 Fairlet 的概念结合了公平性约束。迄今为止，人们已经从多个角度研究了相应的公平相关聚类问题，但迄今为止缺乏从参数化复杂性范式进行详细分析。我们通过在各种结构图参数化（包括树宽、树深和顶点覆盖数）下提供问题的易处理结果来缩小这一差距；考虑到问题在严格受限的输入下的 NP 难度，我们的结果处于可处理性的边缘。
> **Abstract**: We study the generalization of Correlation Clustering which incorporates fairness constraints via the notion of fairlets. The corresponding Fair Correlation Clustering problem has been studied from several perspectives to date, but has so far lacked a detailed analysis from the parameterized complexity paradigm. We close this gap by providing tractability results for the problem under a variety of structural graph parameterizations, including treewidth, treedepth and the vertex cover number; our results lie at the very edge of tractability given the known NP-hardness of the problem on severely restricted inputs.

【4】Memory Reallocation with Polylogarithmic Overhead
- **标题**: 具有多对数开销的内存重新分配
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15417
> **作者**: Ce Jin
> **摘要**: 内存重新分配问题要求动态维护各种大小的给定对象对不重叠的连续内存块的分配，同时支持在线方式的更新（插入/删除）。任何时候活动对象的总大小保证最多为总内存的 $1-ε$ 部分。为了处理在线更新，分配器可能会重新排列内存中的对象以腾出空间，并且此更新的开销定义为移动对象的总大小除以插入/删除的对象的大小。我们的主要结果是一个具有最坏情况预期开销 $\mathrm{polylog}(ε^{-1})$ 的分配器。这成倍地改善了 Farach-Colton、Kuszmaul、Sheffield 和 Westover (2024) 之前实现的最坏情况预期开销 $\tilde O(ε^{-1/2})$，缩小了与 $Ω(\logε^{-1/2})$ 下限的差距。我们的改进基于 Erdős 和 Sárközy (1992) 先前在子集和的背景下使用的向日葵引理的应用。我们的分配器仅在预期中实现多对数开销，并且有时执行昂贵的重建。我们的第二个技术结果表明这是必要的：不可能以高概率实现次多项式开销。
> **Abstract**: The Memory Reallocation problem asks to dynamically maintain an assignment of given objects of various sizes to non-overlapping contiguous chunks of memory, while supporting updates (insertions/deletions) in an online fashion. The total size of live objects at any time is guaranteed to be at most a $1-ε$ fraction of the total memory. To handle an online update, the allocator may rearrange the objects in memory to make space, and the overhead for this update is defined as the total size of moved objects divided by the size of the object being inserted/deleted. Our main result is an allocator with worst-case expected overhead $\mathrm{polylog}(ε^{-1})$. This exponentially improves the previous worst-case expected overhead $\tilde O(ε^{-1/2})$ achieved by Farach-Colton, Kuszmaul, Sheffield, and Westover (2024), narrowing the gap towards the $Ω(\logε^{-1})$ lower bound. Our improvement is based on an application of the sunflower lemma previously used by Erdős and Sárközy (1992) in the context of subset sums. Our allocator achieves polylogarithmic overhead only in expectation, and sometimes performs expensive rebuilds. Our second technical result shows that this is necessary: it is impossible to achieve subpolynomial overhead with high probability.

【5】Testing Monotonicity of Real-Valued Functions on DAGs
- **标题**: 测试 DAG 上实值函数的单调性
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15341
> **作者**: Yuichi Yoshida
> **摘要**: 我们研究具有 $n$ 个顶点的有向无环图 (DAG) 上实值函数的单调性测试。对于每个常数 $δ>0$，我们在 DAG 上针对非自适应双面测试器证明 $Ω(n^{1/2-δ}/\sqrt{\varepsilon})$ 下界，几乎匹配经典的 $O(\sqrt{n/\varepsilon})$ 查询上限。对于常数 $\varepsilon$，我们还证明了显式二分 DAG 上随机自适应单侧测试器的 $Ω(\sqrt n)$ 下界，而之前仅知道 $Ω(\log n)$ 下界。两个下界的一个关键技术要素是正匹配的 Ruzsa-Szemerédi 家族。在算法方面，我们给出简单的非自适应单边测试器，查询复杂度为 $O(\sqrt{m\,\ell}/(\varepsilon n))$ 和 $O(m^{1/3}/\varepsilon^{2/3})$，其中 $m$ 是传递归约中的边数，$\ell$ 是传递闭包中的边数。对于常数 $\varepsilon>0$，当 $m\ell=o(n^3)$ 和 $m=o(n^{3/2})$ 时，这些分别比之前的 $O(\sqrt{n/\varepsilon})$ 界限有所改进。
> **Abstract**: We study monotonicity testing of real-valued functions on directed acyclic graphs (DAGs) with $n$ vertices. For every constant $δ>0$, we prove a $Ω(n^{1/2-δ}/\sqrt{\varepsilon})$ lower bound against non-adaptive two-sided testers on DAGs, nearly matching the classical $O(\sqrt{n/\varepsilon})$-query upper bound. For constant $\varepsilon$, we also prove an $Ω(\sqrt n)$ lower bound for randomized adaptive one-sided testers on explicit bipartite DAGs, whereas previously only an $Ω(\log n)$ lower bound was known. A key technical ingredient in both lower bounds is positive-matching Ruzsa--Szemerédi families. On the algorithmic side, we give simple non-adaptive one-sided testers with query complexity $O(\sqrt{m\,\ell}/(\varepsilon n))$ and $O(m^{1/3}/\varepsilon^{2/3})$, where $m$ is the number of edges in the transitive reduction and $\ell$ is the number of edges in the transitive closure. For constant $\varepsilon>0$, these improve over the previous $O(\sqrt{n/\varepsilon})$ bound when $m\ell=o(n^3)$ and $m=o(n^{3/2})$, respectively.

【6】Revisiting the Sparse Matrix Compression Problem
- **标题**: 重新审视稀疏矩阵压缩问题
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15314
> **作者**: Vincent Jugé,Dominik Köppl,Vincent Limouzy,Andrea Marino,Jannik Olblich,Giulia Punzi,Takeaki Uno
> **摘要**: 稀疏矩阵压缩问题要求二进制 $n \times \ell$ 矩阵的一维表示，该表示由行索引的整数数组和每行的移位函数组成，以便通过查阅该表示在恒定时间内访问矩阵条目是可能的。已经证明，寻找长度为 $\ell+ρ$ 的整数数组或将移位函数限制为 $ρ$ 值的决策问题是 NP 完全的（参见 Garey 和 Johnson 的教科书）。作为一种实用的启发式方法，提出了一种贪婪算法来移动第 $i$ 行，直到它与其前驱行形成解决方案。尽管这种贪心算法在实践中因其良好的近似性而受到重视，但我们证明它实际上表现出 $ θ(\sqrt{\ell+ρ})$ 的近似率。我们给出了参数化的进一步硬度结果，例如不同行的数量或每行非零条目的最大数量。最后，我们设计了一种 DP 算法来解决双对数矩阵宽度或对数宽度的进一步限制问题。我们还在新的视角下通过引入问题的变体来研究所有这些发现，其中我们希望通过修剪非零边界来最小化所得整数数组的长度，这在文献中尚未研究过，但具有实际动机。
> **Abstract**: The sparse matrix compression problem asks for a one-dimensional representation of a binary $n \times \ell$ matrix, formed by an integer array of row indices and a shift function for each row, such that accessing a matrix entry is possible in constant time by consulting this representation. It has been shown that the decision problem for finding an integer array of length $\ell+ρ$ or restricting the shift function up to values of $ρ$ is NP-complete (cf. the textbook of Garey and Johnson). As a practical heuristic, a greedy algorithm has been proposed to shift the $i$-th row until it forms a solution with its predecessor rows. Despite that this greedy algorithm is cherished for its good approximation in practice, we show that it actually exhibits an approximation ratio of $Θ(\sqrt{\ell+ρ})$. We give further hardness results for parameterizations such as the number of distinct rows or the maximum number of non-zero entries per row. Finally, we devise a DP-algorithm that solves the problem for double-logarithmic matrix widths or logarithmic widths for further restrictions. We study all these findings also under a new perspective by introducing a variant of the problem, where we wish to minimize the length of the resulting integer array by trimming the non-zero borders, which has not been studied in the literature before but has practical motivations.

【7】Near-real-time Solutions for Online String Problems
- **标题**: 在线字符串问题的近实时解决方案
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15311
> **作者**: Dominik Köppl,Gregory Kucherov
> **摘要**: 基于 Breslauer-Italiano 在线后缀树构建算法（2013），对每个字母的更新时间提供双对数最坏情况保证，我们为字符串上的几个经典问题开发了近实时算法，包括最长重复后缀数组的计算、（反向）Lempel-Ziv 77 分解以及最小唯一子字符串的维护，所有这些都以在线方式进行。我们的解决方案在每个字母的最坏情况时间方面改进了这些问题的最著名的运行时间，为此我们在线性空间内实现了多对数时间复杂度。这些问题的最著名结果需要每个字母的多对数时间复杂度或仅提供摊余复杂度范围。由于独立兴趣，我们根据它们的不可约表示在空间和时间范围内给出最长的先前因子数组和最长的重复后缀数组之间的转换，其大小​​可以与输入字符串的长度呈次线性关系。
> **Abstract**: Based on the Breslauer-Italiano online suffix tree construction algorithm (2013) with double logarithmic worst-case guarantees on the update time per letter, we develop near-real-time algorithms for several classical problems on strings, including the computation of the longest repeating suffix array, the (reversed) Lempel-Ziv 77 factorization, and the maintenance of minimal unique substrings, all in an online manner. Our solutions improve over the best known running times for these problems in terms of the worst-case time per letter, for which we achieve a poly-log-logarithmic time complexity, within a linear space. Best known results for these problems require a poly-logarithmic time complexity per letter or only provide amortized complexity bounds. As a result of independent interest, we give conversions between the longest previous factor array and the longest repeating suffix array in space and time bounds based on their irreducible representations, which can have sizes sublinear in the length of the input string.

【8】Expander Decomposition with Almost Optimal Overhead
- **标题**: 具有几乎最佳开销的扩展器分解
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15015
> **作者**: Nikhil Bansal,Arun Jambulapati,Thatchaphol Saranurak
> **摘要**: 我们提出了第一个用于计算近乎最优的\emph{flow}-expander分解的多项式时间算法。给定图 $G$ 和参数 $φ$，我们的算法最多删除 $φ\log^{1+o(1)}n$ 部分边，以便每个剩余的连接组件都是 $φ$-\emph{flow}-expander（比 $φ$-\emph{cut}-expander 更有力的保证）。这实现了开销 $\log^{1+o(1)}n$，几乎匹配已经适用于剪切扩展器分解的 $Ω(\log n)$ 图论下界，最高可达 $\log^{o(1)}n$ 因子。先前的多项式时间算法需要删除 $O(φ\log^{1.5}n)$ 和 $O(φ\log^{2}n)$ 部分边，以分别保证 $φ$-cut-expander 和 $φ$-flow-expander 分量。
> **Abstract**: We present the first polynomial-time algorithm for computing a near-optimal \emph{flow}-expander decomposition. Given a graph $G$ and a parameter $φ$, our algorithm removes at most a $φ\log^{1+o(1)}n$ fraction of edges so that every remaining connected component is a $φ$-\emph{flow}-expander (a stronger guarantee than being a $φ$-\emph{cut}-expander). This achieves overhead $\log^{1+o(1)}n$, nearly matching the $Ω(\log n)$ graph-theoretic lower bound that already holds for cut-expander decompositions, up to a $\log^{o(1)}n$ factor. Prior polynomial-time algorithms required removing $O(φ\log^{1.5}n)$ and $O(φ\log^{2}n)$ fractions of edges to guarantee $φ$-cut-expander and $φ$-flow-expander components, respectively.

【9】On the Parameterized Tractability of Packing Vertex-Disjoint A-Paths with Length Constraints
- **标题**: 具有长度约束的打包顶点不相交A路径的参数化可处理性
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14768
> **作者**: Susobhan Bandopadhyay,Aritra Banik,Diptapriyo Majumdar,Abhishek Sahu
> **摘要**: 给定一个无向图 G 和一个集合 A \subseteq V(G)，A 路径是 G 中的一条路径，起始和结束于 A 的两个不同顶点，中间顶点在 V(G) \setminus A 中。如果路径的长度恰好为 \ell，则 A 路径称为 (A,\ell) 路径。在{\sc (A, \ell)-路径打包}问题（ALPP）中，我们试图确定 G 中是否存在 k 个顶点不相交的（A, \ell）路径。我们通过结构参数来解决这个问题。我们证明当 ALPP 通过到路径的组合参数距离 (dtp) 和 |A| 进行参数化时，它是 W[1]-hard。此外，我们考虑组合参数到簇的距离 (cvd) + |A|和到簇的距离 (cvd) + \ell。对于这两个组合参数，我们提供 FPT 算法。最后，我们将顶点覆盖数 (vc) 视为参数，并提供具有 O(vc^2) 个顶点的内核。
> **Abstract**: Given an undirected graph G and a set A \subseteq V(G), an A-path is a path in G that starts and ends at two distinct vertices of A with intermediate vertices in V(G) \setminus A. An A-path is called an (A,\ell)-path if the length of the path is exactly \ell. In the {\sc (A, \ell)-Path Packing} problem (ALPP), we seek to determine whether there exist k vertex-disjoint (A, \ell)-paths in G or not. We pursue this problem with respect to structural parameters. We prove that ALPP is W[1]-hard when it is parameterized by the combined parameter distance to path (dtp) and |A|. In addition, we consider the combined parameters distance to cluster (cvd) + |A| and distance to cluster (cvd) + \ell. For both these combined parameters, we provide FPT algorithms. Finally, we consider the vertex cover number (vc) as the parameter and provide a kernel with O(vc^2) vertices.

【10】Near-Linear Time Computation of Welzl Orders on Graphs with Linear Neighborhood Complexity
- **标题**: 具有线性邻域复杂度的图上 Welzl 阶的近线性时间计算
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14625
> **作者**: Jan Dreier,Clemens Kuske
> **摘要**: Welzl 引入的低交叉数阶是范围搜索和计算几何中的基本工具。最近，他们在结构图论中发现了重要的应用：具有线性破碎函数的集合系统对应于具有线性邻域复杂性的图类。对于此类系统，韦尔茨尔定理保证存在仅具有 $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 n)$ 交叉的阶。一系列工作逐渐改进了计算此类阶数的运行时间，从 Chazelle 和 Welzl 最初的 $\mathcal{O}(|U|^3 |\mathcal{F}|)$ 界限，到 Har-Peled 的 $\mathcal{O}(|U|^2|\mathcal{F}|)$，到最近 Csikós 和 Mustafa 的基于采样的方法。我们提出了一种随机算法，用于计算具有线性原始和对偶粉碎函数的集合系统的 Welzl 阶，时间 $\mathcal{O}(\|S\| \log \|S\|)$，其中 $\|S\| =|U| + \sum_{X \in \mathcal{F}} |X|$ 是规范输入表示的大小。作为一个应用程序，我们在时间上计算具有（近）线性邻域复杂度的图类中的紧凑邻域覆盖，并将单子稳定图类的一阶模型检查的运行时间从 $\mathcal{O}(n^{5+\varepsilon})$ 提高到 $\mathcal{O}(n^{3+\varepsilon})$。
> **Abstract**: Orders with low crossing number, introduced by Welzl, are a fundamental tool in range searching and computational geometry. Recently, they have found important applications in structural graph theory: set systems with linear shatter functions correspond to graph classes with linear neighborhood complexity. For such systems, Welzl's theorem guarantees the existence of orders with only $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 n)$ crossings. A series of works has progressively improved the runtime for computing such orders, from Chazelle and Welzl's original $\mathcal{O}(|U|^3 |\mathcal{F}|)$ bound, through Har-Peled's $\mathcal{O}(|U|^2|\mathcal{F}|)$, to the recent sampling-based methods of Csikós and Mustafa. We present a randomized algorithm that computes Welzl orders for set systems with linear primal and dual shatter functions in time $\mathcal{O}(\|S\| \log \|S\|)$, where $\|S\| = |U| + \sum_{X \in \mathcal{F}} |X|$ is the size of the canonical input representation. As an application, we compute compact neighborhood covers in graph classes with (near-)linear neighborhood complexity in time \(\mathcal{O}(n \log n)\) and improve the runtime of first-order model checking on monadically stable graph classes from $\mathcal{O}(n^{5+\varepsilon})$ to $\mathcal{O}(n^{3+\varepsilon})$.

【11】Faster Pseudo-Deterministic Minimum Cut
- **标题**: 更快的伪确定性最小割
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14550
> **作者**: Yotam Kenneth-Mordoch
> **摘要**: 伪确定性算法是随机算法，具有高恒定概率，输出固定的规范解。最近，Agarwala 和 Varma [ITCS'26] 发起了针对全局最小割问题的伪确定性算法的研究，他们提出了一种黑盒归约，其开销为 $O(\log n \log \log n)$ 。我们引入了一种自然的图论打破平局机制，该机制唯一地选择规范最小割。使用这种机制，我们获得： (i) 一种用于加权图的伪确定性最小割算法，运行时间为 $O(m\log^2 n)$，消除了先前工作的 $O(\log n \log \log n)$ 开销，并匹配现有的随机算法。 (ii) 第一个伪确定性算法，用于在完全动态的未加权图中维护规范最小割，具有 $\mathrm{polylog}(n)$ 更新时间和 $\tilde{O}(n)$ 查询时间。 (iii) 改进动态流和剪切查询计算模型中未加权图的伪确定性算法，匹配最佳随机算法。
> **Abstract**: Pseudo-deterministic algorithms are randomized algorithms that, with high constant probability, output a fixed canonical solution. The study of pseudo-deterministic algorithms for the global minimum cut problem was recently initiated by Agarwala and Varma [ITCS'26], who gave a black-box reduction incurring an $O(\log n \log \log n)$ overhead. We introduce a natural graph-theoretic tie-breaking mechanism that uniquely selects a canonical minimum cut. Using this mechanism, we obtain: (i) A pseudo-deterministic minimum cut algorithm for weighted graphs running in $O(m\log^2 n)$ time, eliminating the $O(\log n \log \log n)$ overhead of prior work and matching existing randomized algorithms. (ii) The first pseudo-deterministic algorithm for maintaining a canonical minimum cut in a fully-dynamic unweighted graph, with $\mathrm{polylog}(n)$ update time and $\tilde{O}(n)$ query time. (iii) Improved pseudo-deterministic algorithms for unweighted graphs in the dynamic streaming and cut-query models of computation, matching the best randomized algorithms.

【12】Sensitivity of Repetitiveness Measures to String Reversal
- **标题**: 重复性测量对字符串反转的敏感性
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14385
> **作者**: Hideo Bannai,Yuto Fujie,Peaker Guo,Shunsuke Inenaga,Yuto Nakashima,Simon J. Puglisi,Cristian Urbina
> **摘要**: 我们研究了字符串反转对几种重复性测量的影响。首先，我们展示了一个无限的字符串族，其中 Burrows-Wheeler 变换 (BWT) 游程长度编码中的游程数量 $r$ 在反转字符串时可以额外增加 $θ(n)$。这大大提高了 $r$ 的加性灵敏度的已知 $Ω(\log n)$ 下界，并且它是渐近紧的。我们将结果推广到 BWT 的其他变体，包括带有附加字符串结尾符号的变体和双射 BWT。我们表明，类似的结果适用于文本的 Lempel--Ziv 77 (LZ) 解析的大小 $z$，也适用于它的一些变体，包括非重叠 LZ 解析和 LZ 端解析。此外，我们将比率 $z(w^R)/z(w)$ 从下面接近 $3$ 的字符串族描述为 $|w|\rightarrow \infty$。我们还展示了最小字典法解析的大小 $v$ 对字符串反转的加性敏感性 $θ(n)$ 的渐近紧下界。最后，我们证明 $v$ 对反转字符串的乘法敏感度是 $θ(\log n)$，并且这个下界也是紧的。总的来说，我们的结果暴露了在实践中广泛使用的重复性测量的局限性，以防止字符串反转（一种简单而自然的数据转换）。
> **Abstract**: We study the impact that string reversal can have on several repetitiveness measures. First, we exhibit an infinite family of strings where the number, $r$, of runs in the run-length encoding of the Burrows--Wheeler transform (BWT) can increase additively by $Θ(n)$ when reversing the string. This substantially improves the known $Ω(\log n)$ lower-bound for the additive sensitivity of $r$ and it is asymptotically tight. We generalize our result to other variants of the BWT, including the variant with an appended end-of-string symbol and the bijective BWT. We show that an analogous result holds for the size $z$ of the Lempel--Ziv 77 (LZ) parsing of the text, and also for some of its variants, including the non-overlapping LZ parsing, and the LZ-end parsing. Moreover, we describe a family of strings for which the ratio $z(w^R)/z(w)$ approaches $3$ from below as $|w|\rightarrow \infty$. We also show an asymptotically tight lower-bound of $Θ(n)$ for the additive sensitivity of the size $v$ of the smallest lexicographic parsing to string reversal. Finally, we show that the multiplicative sensitivity of $v$ to reversing the string is $Θ(\log n)$, and this lower-bound is also tight. Overall, our results expose the limitations of repetitiveness measures that are widely used in practice, against string reversal -- a simple and natural data transformation.

## 新兴技术(cs.ET:Emerging Technologies)

【1】Quantum Computing for Healthcare Digital Twin Systems
- **标题**: 医疗保健数字孪生系统的量子计算
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15477
> **作者**: Asma Taheri Monfared,Andrea Bombarda,Angelo Gargantini,Majid Haghparast
> **摘要**: 医疗保健系统日益复杂，需要先进的计算模型来进行实时监控、安全数据交换和智能决策。数字孪生 (DT) 提供物理医疗保健实体的虚拟表示，从而实现持续的患者监控和个性化护理。然而，经典的DT框架在可扩展性、计算效率和安全性方面面临限制。最近的研究引入了量子数字孪生 (QDT)，通过量子计算提高性能，解决医疗保健环境中的抗量子安全性和高效任务卸载等挑战。尽管取得了这些进步，大多数现有的 QDT 模型仍然受到与量子硬件限制、混合经典量子系统集成、基于云的量子访问、可扩展性和临床信任相关的基本挑战的限制。本文对医疗保健领域的 QDT 进行了全面回顾，特别侧重于识别和分析目前阻碍其在现实世界中采用的主要挑战。此外，它还概述了关键研究方向和支持策略，旨在推动下一代医疗保健应用的安全、可靠和临床可行的量子数字孪生系统的开发。
> **Abstract**: The growing complexity of healthcare systems requires advanced computational models for real-time monitoring, secure data exchange, and intelligent decision-making. Digital Twins (DTs) provide virtual representations of physical healthcare entities, enabling continuous patient monitoring and personalized care. However, classical DT frameworks face limitations in scalability, computational efficiency, and security. Recent studies have introduced Quantum Digital Twins (QDTs) to enhance performance through quantum computing, addressing challenges such as quantum-resistant security and efficient task offloading in healthcare environments. Despite these advances, most existing QDT models remain constrained by fundamental challenges related to quantum hardware limitations, hybrid classical-quantum system integration, cloud-based quantum access, scalability, and clinical trust. This paper provides a comprehensive review of QDTs for healthcare, with a particular focus on identifying and analyzing the key challenges that currently hinder their real-world adoption. Furthermore, it outlines critical research directions and enabling strategies aimed at advancing the development of secure, reliable, and clinically viable quantum digital twin systems for next-generation healthcare applications.

【2】Quantum Optimization for Access Point Selection Under Budget Constraint
- **标题**: 预算约束下接入点选择的量子优化
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15049
> **作者**: Mohamed Khalil Brik,Ahmed Shokry,Moustafa Youssef
> **摘要**: 最佳接入点（AP）选择对于准确的室内定位至关重要，但它受到预算的限制，需要在定位精度和部署成本之间进行权衡。经典的 AP 选择方法通常计算成本高昂，阻碍了它们在大规模 3D 室内环境中的应用。在本文中，我们介绍了一种预算约束下的量子 AP 选择算法。所提出的算法利用量子退火来识别给定预算内允许的最有效的 AP 子集。我们将 AP 选择问题表述为二次无约束二元优化 (QUBO) 问题，使其适合量子退火求解器。所提出的技术可以大大降低基础设施要求，而对性能的影响可以忽略不计。我们实现了所提出的量子算法并将其部署在现实的 3D 测试台中。我们的结果表明，所提出的方法可以将所需的 AP 数量减少 96.1%，同时保持相当的 3D 定位精度。此外，所提出的量子方法在准确性和计算速度方面都优于经典的 AP 选择算法。具体来说，我们的技术实现了 0.20 秒的时间，比经典技术加速了 61 倍，同时与经典技术相比，平均定位误差降低了 10%。对于楼层定位，量子方法实现了 73% 的楼层准确率，优于经典的 AP 选择 (58.6%)，甚至优于使用完整的 AP 集 (70.4%)。这凸显了所提出的量子 AP 选择算法对于大规模 3D 定位的前景。
> **Abstract**: Optimal Access Point (AP) selection is crucial for accurate indoor localization, yet it is constrained by budget, creating a trade-off between localization accuracy and deployment cost. Classical approaches to AP selection are often computationally expensive, hindering their application in large-scale 3D indoor environments. In this paper, we introduce a quantum APs selection algorithm under a budget constraint. The proposed algorithm leverages quantum annealing to identify the most effective subset of APs allowed within a given budget. We formulate the APs selection problem as a quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) problem, making it suitable for quantum annealing solvers. The proposed technique can drastically reduce infrastructure requirements with a negligible impact on performance. We implement the proposed quantum algorithm and deploy it in a realistic 3D testbed. Our results show that the proposed approach can reduce the number of required APs by 96.1% while maintaining a comparable 3D localization accuracy. Furthermore, the proposed quantum approach outperforms classical AP selection algorithms in both accuracy and computational speed. Specifically, our technique achieves a time of 0.20 seconds, representing a speedup of 61 times over its classical counterpart, while reducing the mean localization error by 10% compared to the classical counterpart. For floor localization, the quantum approach achieves 73% floor accuracy, outperforming both the classical AP selection (58.6%) and even using the complete set of APs (70.4%). This highlights the promise of the proposed quantum APs selection algorithm for large-scale 3D localization.

【3】Full-Field Damage Monitoring in Architected Lattices Using In situ Electrical Impedance Tomography
- **标题**: 使用原位电阻抗断层扫描对架构晶格进行全场损伤监测
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15048
> **作者**: Akash Deep,Andrea Samore,Alistair McEwan,Andrew McBride,Shanmugam Kumar
> **摘要**: 电阻抗断层扫描 (EIT) 可实现内部电导率分布的非侵入性、空间连续重建，提供超越传统点测量的全场感测。在此，我们报告了在可调谐架构晶格材料框架内首次原位实施 EIT，从而能够在广泛的晶格设计空间中进行系统探索，同时实现对 3D 打印多功能晶格复合材料中的损伤演变（包括早期阶段、预断裂事件）的实时监控。晶格是通过基于 Voronoi 的分支主干分支图案设计的，灵感来自 2D 壁纸对称性，并使用注入 CNT 的光固化树脂制造，并通过场发射扫描电子显微镜证实了纳米级填料的分散。沿晶格外围分布的 16 个电极可在准静态拉伸负载期间进行 EIT 测量。使用相邻和跨电流注入方案重建的电导率图以高时间分辨率解决连续韧带断裂，局部电导率损失在数量上与断裂部位（包括远离电极的区域）一致。架构可调性允许系统控制 EIT 成像对早期损坏的敏感性，而故障时明显的电阻不连续性进一步证实了空间定位；全局端到端电阻测量补充了宏观应力应变响应。总的来说，这些结果将原位 EIT 确立为一种可扩展的全场传感模式，适用于建筑多功能材料，为实现自主、智能材料和数据丰富的材料状态提供了一条经过实验验证的途径，可以为结构、生物医学和能源相关应用的数字孪生框架提供信息。
> **Abstract**: Electrical impedance tomography (EIT) enables non-invasive, spatially continuous reconstruction of internal conductivity distributions, providing full field sensing beyond conventional point measurements. Here, we report the first in situ implementation of EIT within a tunable architected lattice materials framework, enabling systematic exploration across a broad lattice design space while achieving real time monitoring of damage evolution, including early stage, prefracture events, in 3D printed multifunctional lattice composites. Lattices are designed via Voronoi based branch trunk branch motifs inspired by 2D wallpaper symmetries and fabricated using CNT infused photocurable resins, with nanoscale filler dispersion confirmed by field emission scanning electron microscopy. Sixteen electrodes distributed along the lattice periphery enable EIT measurements during quasi static tensile loading. Conductivity maps reconstructed using adjacent and across current injection schemes resolve sequential ligament fracture with high temporal resolution, with localised conductivity loss quantitatively coinciding with fracture sites, including regions remote from electrodes. Architectural tunability allows systematic control of EIT imaging sensitivity to early stage damage, while pronounced resistance discontinuities at failure further corroborate spatial localisation; global end to end resistance measurements complement macroscopic stress strain responses. Collectively, these results establish in situ EIT as a scalable, full field sensing modality for architected multifunctional materials, providing an experimentally validated pathway toward autonomous, intelligent materials and data rich material states that can inform digital twin frameworks for structural, biomedical, and energy related applications.

【4】High Convergence Rates of CMOS Invertible Logic Circuits Based on Many-Body Hamiltonians
- **标题**: 基于多体哈密顿量的CMOS可逆逻辑电路的高收敛性
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15033
> **作者**: Naoya Onizawa,Takahiro Hanyu
> **摘要**: 本文介绍了基于多体哈密顿量的 CMOS 可逆逻辑 (CIL) 电路。 CIL 可以通过使用随机计算对相应的哈密顿量进行退火来实现函数的概率前向和后向运算。我们创建了一个哈密顿量，其中包括自旋的三体相互作用（概率节点）。它提供了一定程度的自由度来设计比传统二体哈密顿量更简单的哈密顿量（能量）景观。更简单的景观使得更容易达到全球最低能量。所提出的三体 CIL 电路是用传统的两体 CIL 电路进行设计和评估的，从而使收敛速度提高几倍，同时 FPGA 上的面积开销可以忽略不计。
> **Abstract**: This paper introduces CMOS invertible-logic (CIL) circuits based on many-body Hamiltonians. CIL can realize probabilistic forward and backward operations of a function by annealing a corresponding Hamiltonian using stochastic computing. We have created a Hamiltonian that includes three-body interaction of spins (probabilistic nodes). It provides some degrees of freedom to design a simpler landscape of Hamiltonian (energy) than that of the conventional two-body Hamiltonian. The simpler landscape makes it easier to reach the global minimum energy. The proposed three-body CIL circuits are designed and evaluated with the conventional two-body CIL circuits, resulting in few-times higher convergence rates with negligible area overhead on FPGA.

【5】Pairwise XOR and XNOR Gates in Squeezed Instantaneous Noise Based Logic
- **标题**: 基于压缩瞬时噪声的逻辑中的成对异或门和异或非门
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15032
> **作者**: Nasir Kenarangui,Laszlo B. Kish,Arthur Powalka
> **摘要**: 基于瞬时噪声的逻辑（INBL）是一种新颖的计算方法，它使用随机过程对二进制信息进行编码。它使用 M 个噪声位的 2M 个正交随机参考噪声来构造一个维度为 2^M 的指数大希尔伯特空间（超空间）。 INBL 为特定问题提供了量子式并行性的经典替代方案，与经典算法相比具有指数级加速。基于最近引入为对称 INBL 方案定义的成对 XOR 和 XNOR 运算的工作，本文为压缩 INBL 方案实现了这些门。超空间向量是与M位长的二进制数对应的乘积串。所提出的操作可以成对应用于超空间向量及其叠加，同时保持与压缩参考系统的兼容性。我们验证了压缩方案 XOR/XNOR 门运算在按位和目标 M 位字符串上具有正确的布尔行为，并证明该运算保留了瞬时求值。结果表明，之前为对称 INBL 开发的 XOR/XNOR 工具包可以针对压缩方案进行定制。这一开发是压缩 INBL 方案中更复杂的 INBL 算法所需的门集的关键部分，并推进了 INBL 中门通用性的目标。它进一步强化了 INBL 作为灵活的经典计算框架的理由，可以模拟量子计算的一些结构优势。
> **Abstract**: Instantaneous noise-based logic (INBL) is a novel computing approach that encodes binary information using stochastic processes. It uses 2M orthogonal stochastic reference noises for M noise-bits to construct an exponentially large Hilbert space (hyperspace) of dimension 2^M. INBL offers a classical alternative to quantum-style parallelism for specific problems with exponential speedup compared to classical algorithms. Building on recent work that introduced pairwise XOR and XNOR operations defined for a symmetric INBL scheme, this paper implements these gates for a squeezed INBL scheme. Hyperspace vectors are product strings corresponding to M-bit long binary numbers. The proposed operations can apply pairwise on hyperspace vectors and their superpositions, while remaining compatible with the squeezed reference system. We validate that the squeezed-scheme XOR/XNOR gate operations have correct Boolean behavior over both bitwise and targeted M-bit strings and demonstrate that the operations preserve instantaneous evaluation. The results show that the XOR/XNOR toolkit, previously developed for symmetric INBL, can be tailored for the squeezed scheme. This development is a key part of the gate set needed for more complex INBL algorithms in the squeezed INBL scheme and advances the objective of gate universality in INBL. It further strengthens the case for INBL as a flexible, classical computing framework that can emulate some structural advantages of quantum computation.

## 形式语言和自动机理论(cs.FL:Formal Languages and Automata Theory)

【1】Constant-Time Dynamic Enumeration of Word Infixes in a Regular Language
- **标题**: 正则语言中单词中缀的恒定时间动态枚举
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14748
> **作者**: Antoine Amarilli,Sven Dziadek,Luc Segoufin
> **摘要**: 对于固定的正则语言 $L$，$L$中缀的枚举是以下任务：给定一个输入词 $w = a_1 \cdots a_n$，我们必须枚举属于 $L$ 的 $w$ 的中缀，即 $i \leq j$ 对，使得 $a_i \cdots a_j \in L$。我们对 $L$ 中缀的动态枚举感兴趣，其中我们必须另外支持 $w$ 上的字母替换更新（例如，“用字母 $a$ 替换 $w$ 的第 $i$ 个字母”）。每次更新都会更改要枚举的中缀集，并重置枚举状态。我们研究了哪些常规语言 $L$ 可以在恒定延迟（即下一个中缀总是在恒定时间内生成）和整个枚举过程中恒定的附加内存中执行 $L$ 中缀的动态枚举，同时支持恒定时间内的每次更新。我们证明，对于带有中性字母的语言 $L$，如果语言 $L$ 属于 ZG 类并且是可扩展的（即，如果 $u \in L$ 和 $u$ 是 $v$ 的因数，则 $v \in L$），则可以使用确保恒定时间更新和恒定延迟的简单算法来实现 $L$ 中缀的动态枚举，该算法确保恒定时间更新和恒定延迟，但不能保证恒定附加内存。我们的主要贡献是展示一种仅使用恒定附加内存的算法，并适用于更一般的半可扩展 ZG 语言，我们为此给出了几个等效的特征。我们进一步讨论我们的结果是否可以推广到更大的语言类别并显示一些（条件）下限。
> **Abstract**: For a fixed regular language $L$, the enumeration of $L$-infixes is the following task: we are given an input word $w = a_1 \cdots a_n$ and we must enumerate the infixes of $w$ that belong to $L$, i.e., the pairs $i \leq j$ such that $a_i \cdots a_j \in L$. We are interested in dynamic enumeration of $L$-infixes, where we must additionally support letter substitution updates on $w$ (e.g., "replace the $i$-th letter of $w$ by a letter $a$"). Each update changes the set of infixes to enumerate, and resets the enumeration state. We study for which regular languages $L$ we can perform dynamic enumeration of $L$-infixes in constant delay (i.e., the next infix is always produced in constant time) and constant additional memory throughout the enumeration, while supporting each update in constant time. We show that, for languages $L$ with a neutral letter, if the language $L$ belongs to the class ZG and is extensible (i.e., if $u \in L$ and $u$ is a factor of $v$ then $v \in L$), then dynamic enumeration of $L$-infixes can be achieved with a simple algorithm that ensures constant-time updates and constant delay, but not constant additional memory. Our main contribution is then to show an algorithm that additionally uses only constant additional memory, and applies to a more general class of semi-extensible ZG languages for which we give several equivalent characterizations. We further discuss whether our results can be generalized to larger language classes and show some (conditional) lower bounds.

## 计算机科学与博弈论(cs.GT:Computer Science and Game Theory)

【1】Outer Diversity of Structured Domains
- **标题**: 结构化域的外部多样性
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15708
> **作者**: Piotr Faliszewski,Krzysztof Sornat,Stanisław Szufa,Tomasz Wąs
> **摘要**: 序数偏好域是允许选民在选举中进行投票的偏好顺序的子集。我们介绍和研究域的外部多样性的概念，并评估其对于许多众所周知的结构化域的价值，例如单峰、单交叉、群可分离和欧几里德域。
> **Abstract**: An ordinal preference domain is a subset of preference orders that the voters are allowed to cast in an election. We introduce and study the notion of outer diversity of a domain and evaluate its value for a number of well-known structured domains, such as the single-peaked, single-crossing, group-separable, and Euclidean ones.

【2】Decision Making under Imperfect Recall: Algorithms and Benchmarks
- **标题**: 不完美召回下的决策：算法和基准
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15252
> **作者**: Emanuel Tewolde,Brian Hu Zhang,Ioannis Anagnostides,Tuomas Sandholm,Vincent Conitzer
> **摘要**: 在博弈论中，不完美回忆决策问题模拟了代理忘记之前持有的信息的情况。它们包括诸如“心不在焉的驾驶员”之类的游戏和沟通有限的团队游戏。在本文中，我们介绍了第一个针对不完美召回决策问题的基准套件。我们的基准测试涵盖了各种问题类型，包括涉及人工智能系统中引发敏感信息的隐私问题，以及通过模拟测试代理来实现人工智能安全的问题。在使用该套件生成的 61 个问题实例中，我们评估了不同算法在此类问题中寻找一阶最优策略的性能。特别是，我们介绍了用于非线性约束优化的后悔匹配（RM）算法系列。这类无参数算法在解决大型两人零和博弈方面取得了巨大成功，但令人惊讶的是，迄今为止，除了该设置之外，它们还没有被探索过。我们的主要发现是，RM 算法始终优于常用的一阶优化器（例如投影梯度下降），通常高出几个数量级。这首次将 RM 系列确立为解决大规模约束优化问题的强大方法。
> **Abstract**: In game theory, imperfect-recall decision problems model situations in which an agent forgets information it held before. They encompass games such as the ``absentminded driver'' and team games with limited communication. In this paper, we introduce the first benchmark suite for imperfect-recall decision problems. Our benchmarks capture a variety of problem types, including ones concerning privacy in AI systems that elicit sensitive information, and AI safety via testing of agents in simulation. Across 61 problem instances generated using this suite, we evaluate the performance of different algorithms for finding first-order optimal strategies in such problems. In particular, we introduce the family of regret matching (RM) algorithms for nonlinear constrained optimization. This class of parameter-free algorithms has enjoyed tremendous success in solving large two-player zero-sum games, but, surprisingly, they were hitherto relatively unexplored beyond that setting. Our key finding is that RM algorithms consistently outperform commonly employed first-order optimizers such as projected gradient descent, often by orders of magnitude. This establishes, for the first time, the RM family as a formidable approach to large-scale constrained optimization problems.

【3】Robust Value Maximization in Challenge the Champ Tournaments with Probabilistic Outcomes
- **标题**: 以概率结果挑战冠军锦标赛的稳健价值最大化
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14966
> **作者**: Umang Bhaskar,Juhi Chaudhary,Sushmita Gupta,Pallavi Jain,Sanjay Seetharaman
> **摘要**: 挑战冠军是一种简单的锦标赛形式，由选手的顺序（称为种子）决定。此顺序中的第一个玩家是初始冠军，并面对下一个玩家。每场比赛的结果决定了当前的冠军，他将面对顺序中的下一位选手。每个选手也都有人气，每场比赛的价值就是胜利者的人气。之前已经研究过当每场比赛都有确定性结果时锦标赛中的价值最大化。然而，比赛结果通常是概率性的，而不是确定性的。我们研究挑战冠军锦标赛中稳健的价值最大化，此时比赛的获胜者可能是有概率的。也就是说，我们寻求最大化所获得的总价值，而不管概率匹配的结果如何。我们表明，即使在简单的二进制设置中，对于非自适应算法，最佳鲁棒值（我们称之为 \textsc{VnaR} 或没有风险的值）也很难近似。然而，如果我们允许自适应算法根据之前比赛的结果确定挑战者的顺序，或者用概率结果限制比赛，我们可以获得最佳 \textsc{VnaR} 的良好近似。
> **Abstract**: Challenge the Champ is a simple tournament format, where an ordering of the players -- called a seeding -- is decided. The first player in this order is the initial champ, and faces the next player. The outcome of each match decides the current champion, who faces the next player in the order. Each player also has a popularity, and the value of each match is the popularity of the winner. Value maximization in tournaments has been previously studied when each match has a deterministic outcome. However, match outcomes are often probabilistic, rather than deterministic. We study robust value maximization in Challenge the Champ tournaments, when the winner of a match may be probabilistic. That is, we seek to maximize the total value that is obtained, irrespective of the outcome of probabilistic matches. We show that even in simple binary settings, for non-adaptive algorithms, the optimal robust value -- which we term the \textsc{VnaR}, or the value not at risk -- is hard to approximate. However, if we allow adaptive algorithms that determine the order of challengers based on the outcomes of previous matches, or restrict the matches with probabilistic outcomes, we can obtain good approximations to the optimal \textsc{VnaR}.

【4】A Bayesian Framework for Human-AI Collaboration: Complementarity and Correlation Neglect
- **标题**: 人类与人工智能协作的贝叶斯框架：互补性和相关性忽略
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14331
> **作者**: Saurabh Amin,Amine Bennouna,Daniel Huttenlocher,Dingwen Kong,Liang Lyu,Asuman Ozdaglar
> **摘要**: 我们开发了人类与人工智能交互的决策理论模型，以研究人工智能辅助何时改善或损害人类决策。人类决策者观察私人信息并接收人工智能系统的建议，但可能会不完美地结合这些信号。我们表明，人工智能辅助的效果分解为两个主要力量：人工智能超出人类已知范围的边际信息价值，以及人类如何使用人工智能建议而产生的行为扭曲。我们分析的核心是对人类和人工智能知识之间信息重叠的微观衡量。我们研究了一种与经验相关的不完美决策形式——相关性忽视——尽管有共同的证据，但人类仍将人工智能的建议视为独立于自己的信息。在这个模型下，我们描述了重叠和人工智能能力如何塑造增强、损伤、互补和自动化之间的人机交互机制，并得出关键见解。
> **Abstract**: We develop a decision-theoretic model of human-AI interaction to study when AI assistance improves or impairs human decision-making. A human decision-maker observes private information and receives a recommendation from an AI system, but may combine these signals imperfectly. We show that the effect of AI assistance decomposes into two main forces: the marginal informational value of the AI beyond what the human already knows, and a behavioral distortion arising from how the human uses the AI's recommendation. Central to our analysis is a micro-founded measure of informational overlap between human and AI knowledge. We study an empirically relevant form of imperfect decision-making -- correlation neglect -- whereby humans treat AI recommendations as independent of their own information despite shared evidence. Under this model, we characterize how overlap and AI capabilities shape the Human-AI interaction regime between augmentation, impairment, complementarity, and automation, and draw key insights.

## 人机交互(cs.HC:Human-Computer Interaction)

【1】Unraveling Entangled Feeds: Rethinking Social Media Design to Enhance User Well-being
- **标题**: 解开纠缠的提要：重新思考社交媒体设计以增强用户福祉
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15745
> **作者**: Ashlee Milton,Dan Runningen,Loren Terveen,Harmanpreet Kaur,Stevie Chancellor
> **摘要**: 社交媒体平台迅速采用算法管理，很少考虑对用户心理健康的潜在危害。我们展示了由 21 名被诊断患有精神疾病的参与者参与的设计研讨会关于他们与社交媒体平台互动的调查结果。我们发现用户会提出因果解释或民间理论来理解他们对算法管理的体验。这些民间理论强调了算法设计的崩溃，我们使用纠缠框架来解释，这是一种用户行为与平台结果在情感层面上脱节的现象。参与者解决纠缠和减轻伤害的设计集中于将他们的参与置于情境中并恢复用户对社交媒体的明确控制。纠缠的概念化和由此产生的设计建议对社交计算和推荐系统研究具有影响，特别是在评估和设计支持用户心理健康的社交媒体平台方面。
> **Abstract**: Social media platforms have rapidly adopted algorithmic curation with little consideration for the potential harm to users' mental well-being. We present findings from design workshops with 21 participants diagnosed with mental illness about their interactions with social media platforms. We find that users develop cause-and-effect explanations, or folk theories, to understand their experiences with algorithmic curation. These folk theories highlight a breakdown in algorithmic design that we explain using the framework of entanglement, a phenomenon where there is a disconnect between users' actions and platform outcomes on an emotional level. Participants' designs to address entanglement and mitigate harms centered on contextualizing their engagement and restoring explicit user control on social media. The conceptualization of entanglement and the resulting design recommendations have implications for social computing and recommender systems research, particularly in evaluating and designing social media platforms that support users' mental well-being.

【2】Beyond Labels: Information-Efficient Human-in-the-Loop Learning using Ranking and Selection Queries
- **标题**: 超越标签：使用排序和选择查询的信息高效的人在环学习
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15738
> **作者**: Belén Martín-Urcelay,Yoonsang Lee,Matthieu R. Bloch,Christopher J. Rozell
> **摘要**: 将人类专业知识集成到机器学习系统中通常会降低专家的作用，使其成为给预言机贴上标签，这种范式限制了交换的信息量，并且无法捕捉人类判断的细微差别。我们通过开发一个人机循环框架来学习具有丰富查询类型（包括项目排名和样本选择）的二元分类器来应对这一挑战。我们首先为这些丰富的查询引入概率人类响应模型，这些查询的动机是通过实验观察到的项目的感知隐式分数与其与未知分类器的距离之间的关系。然后，我们使用这些模型设计主动学习算法，利用丰富的查询来增加每次交互所获得的信息。我们提供了样本复杂性的理论界限，并开发了一种易于处理且计算高效的变分近似。通过对源自众包文字情感和图像美学数据集的模拟注释器进行实验，我们证明了样本复杂性的显着降低。我们进一步扩展主动学习策略来选择最大化信息率的查询，明确地平衡信息价值与注释成本。与传统的仅标签主动学习相比，该算法在单词情感分类任务中减少了超过 57% 的学习时间。
> **Abstract**: Integrating human expertise into machine learning systems often reduces the role of experts to labeling oracles, a paradigm that limits the amount of information exchanged and fails to capture the nuances of human judgment. We address this challenge by developing a human-in-the-loop framework to learn binary classifiers with rich query types, consisting of item ranking and exemplar selection. We first introduce probabilistic human response models for these rich queries motivated by the relationship experimentally observed between the perceived implicit score of an item and its distance to the unknown classifier. Using these models, we then design active learning algorithms that leverage the rich queries to increase the information gained per interaction. We provide theoretical bounds on sample complexity and develop a tractable and computationally efficient variational approximation. Through experiments with simulated annotators derived from crowdsourced word-sentiment and image-aesthetic datasets, we demonstrate significant reductions on sample complexity. We further extend active learning strategies to select queries that maximize information rate, explicitly balancing informational value against annotation cost. This algorithm in the word sentiment classification task reduces learning time by more than 57\% compared to traditional label-only active learning.

【3】How to Disclose? Strategic AI Disclosure in Crowdfunding
- **标题**: 如何披露？众筹中的战略人工智能披露
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15698
> **作者**: Ning Wang,Chen Liang
> **摘要**: 随着人工智能 (AI) 越来越多地融入众筹实践，人工智能参与的战略披露变得至关重要。然而，关于不同披露策略如何影响投资者决策的实证见解仍然有限。借鉴信号理论和亚里士多德的修辞框架，我们研究了强制人工智能披露如何影响众筹绩效，以及实质性信号（人工智能参与程度）和修辞信号（标识/明确性、精神/真实性、悲情/情绪基调）如何调节这些影响。利用 Kickstarter 的强制人工智能披露政策作为自然实验和四个补充在线实验，我们发现强制人工智能披露显着降低了众筹绩效：涉及人工智能的项目筹集的资金下降了 39.8%，支持者数量下降了 23.9%。然而，这种不利影响可以通过披露策略系统地缓解。人工智能的更多参与放大了人工智能披露的负面影响，而高真实性和高明确性则减轻了这些影响。有趣的是，过度积极的情绪基调（策略创建者可能会直觉地采用这种策略来抵消人工智能的怀疑）会适得其反并加剧负面结果。补充随机实验确定了两种潜在机制：感知创造者能力和人工智能清洗问题。实质性信号主要影响能力判断，而修辞信号则通过不同的途径发挥作用：要么单独中介，要么依次两者。这些发现为企业家、平台和政策制定者在高风险投资环境中战略性地管理人工智能透明度提供了理论和实践见解。
> **Abstract**: As artificial intelligence (AI) increasingly integrates into crowdfunding practices, strategic disclosure of AI involvement has become critical. Yet, empirical insights into how different disclosure strategies influence investor decisions remain limited. Drawing on signaling theory and Aristotle's rhetorical framework, we examine how mandatory AI disclosure affects crowdfunding performance and how substantive signals (degree of AI involvement) and rhetorical signals (logos/explicitness, ethos/authenticity, pathos/emotional tone) moderate these effects. Leveraging Kickstarter's mandatory AI disclosure policy as a natural experiment and four supplementary online experiments, we find that mandatory AI disclosure significantly reduces crowdfunding performance: funds raised decline by 39.8% and backer counts by 23.9% for AI-involved projects. However, this adverse effect is systematically moderated by disclosure strategy. Greater AI involvement amplifies the negative effects of AI disclosure, while high authenticity and high explicitness mitigate them. Interestingly, excessive positive emotional tone (a strategy creators might intuitively adopt to counteract AI skepticism) backfires and exacerbates negative outcomes. Supplementary randomized experiments identify two underlying mechanisms: perceived creator competence and AI washing concerns. Substantive signals primarily affect competence judgments, whereas rhetorical signals operate through varied pathways: either mediator alone or both in sequence. These findings provide theoretical and practical insights for entrepreneurs, platforms, and policymakers strategically managing AI transparency in high-stakes investment contexts.

【4】Meflex: A Multi-agent Scaffolding System for Entrepreneurial Ideation Iteration via Nonlinear Business Plan Writing
- **标题**: Meflex：通过非线性商业计划写作进行创业创意迭代的多代理脚手架系统
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15631
> **作者**: Lan Luo,Dongyijie Primo Pan,Junhua Zhu,Muzhi Zhou,Pan Hui
> **摘要**: 商业计划（BP）写作在创业教育中发挥着关键作用，帮助学习者构建、评估和迭代完善他们的想法。然而，传统的 BP 写作仍然是一个僵化的、线性的过程，往往无法反映创业理念的动态和递归本质。这种不匹配对于创业新手来说尤其具有挑战性，他们在发展和完善想法时面临着巨大的认知需求。虽然反思和元反思是培养发散性和聚合性思维的关键策略，但现有的写作工具很少支撑这些高阶过程。为了解决这一差距，我们推出了 Meflex System，这是一种基于大型语言模型 (LLM) 的写作工具，它将 BP 写作支架与非线性想法画布集成在一起，以通过反射和元反射支持迭代构思。我们报告了一项由 30 名参与者参与的探索性用户研究的结果，该研究检查了系统的可用性和认知影响。结果表明，Meflex 有效支撑 BP 写作，通过法学硕士支持的反思促进发散思维，增强元反思意识，同时减少复杂想法发展过程中的认知负担。这些发现凸显了基于法学硕士的非线性写作工具在培养更深入、连贯的创业思维方面的潜力。
> **Abstract**: Business plan (BP) writing plays a key role in entrepreneurship education by helping learners construct, evaluate, and iteratively refine their ideas. However, conventional BP writing remains a rigid, linear process that often fails to reflect the dynamic and recursive nature of entrepreneurial ideation. This mismatch is particularly challenging for novice entrepreneurial students, who struggle with the substantial cognitive demands of developing and refining ideas. While reflection and meta-reflection are critical strategies for fostering divergent and convergent thinking, existing writing tools rarely scaffold these higher-order processes. To address this gap, we present the Meflex System, a large language model (LLM)-based writing tool that integrates BP writing scaffolding with a nonlinear idea canvas to support iterative ideation through reflection and meta-reflection. We report findings from an exploratory user study with 30 participants that examined the system's usability and cognitive impact. Results show that Meflex effectively scaffolds BP writing, promotes divergent thinking through LLM-supported reflection, and enhances meta-reflective awareness while reducing cognitive load during complex idea development. These findings highlight the potential of non-linear LLM-based writing tools to foster deeper and coherent entrepreneurial thinking.

【5】"What Are You Doing?": Effects of Intermediate Feedback from Agentic LLM In-Car Assistants During Multi-Step Processing
- **标题**: “你在做什么？”：多步骤处理过程中 Agentic LLM 车载助理的中间反馈的影响
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15569
> **作者**: Johannes Kirmayr,Raphael Wennmacher,Khanh Huynh,Lukas Stappen,Elisabeth André,Florian Alt
> **摘要**: 自主执行多步骤任务的代理人工智能助手对用户体验提出了开放性问题：此类系统在扩展操作期间应如何传达进度和推理，特别是在驾驶等注意力关键的环境中？我们通过一项受控的混合方法研究 (N=45) 来调查来自代理法学硕士的车载助理的反馈时间和冗长程度，比较计划步骤和中间结果反馈与静默操作与仅最终响应。使用车载语音助手的双任务范例，我们发现中间反馈显着提高了感知速度、信任度和用户体验，同时减少了任务负载——在不同的任务复杂性和交互环境中都会产生影响。访谈进一步揭示了用户对自适应方法的偏好：初始高度透明以建立信任，随后随着系统证明可靠而逐渐减少冗长，并根据任务风险和情境进行调整。我们将我们的实证研究结果转化为对代理助理的反馈时间和冗长程度的设计影响，平衡透明度和效率。
> **Abstract**: Agentic AI assistants that autonomously perform multi-step tasks raise open questions for user experience: how should such systems communicate progress and reasoning during extended operations, especially in attention-critical contexts such as driving? We investigate feedback timing and verbosity from agentic LLM-based in-car assistants through a controlled, mixed-methods study (N=45) comparing planned steps and intermediate results feedback against silent operation with final-only response. Using a dual-task paradigm with an in-car voice assistant, we found that intermediate feedback significantly improved perceived speed, trust, and user experience while reducing task load - effects that held across varying task complexities and interaction contexts. Interviews further revealed user preferences for an adaptive approach: high initial transparency to establish trust, followed by progressively reducing verbosity as systems prove reliable, with adjustments based on task stakes and situational context. We translate our empirical findings into design implications for feedback timing and verbosity in agentic assistants, balancing transparency and efficiency.

【6】Reflecting on 1,000 Social Media Journeys: Generational Patterns in Platform Transition
- **标题**: 反思 1,000 次社交媒体之旅：平台转型中的代际模式
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15489
> **作者**: Artur Solomonik,Nicolas Ruiz,Hendrik Heuer
> **摘要**: 社交媒体拥有数十亿用户，但我们仍然不完全理解为什么用户更喜欢一个平台而不是另一个平台。在已经很受欢迎的竞争对手中建立新平台是很困难的。先前的研究已经丰富地记录了人们在各个平台上的体验，但将这些体验置于用户的整个社交媒体体验中仍然具有挑战性。人们使用过哪些平台，为什么要在这些平台之间转换？我们从 1,000 名美国参与者的配额样本中收集了数据。我们引入\emph{社交媒体之旅}的概念来系统地研究他们的整个社交媒体体验。我们确定社交媒体领域的推力和拉力因素。我们还展示了不同世代如何根据个人需求采用社交媒体平台。通过这项工作，我们在讨论社交媒体技术时转向整体视角，为平台设计、治理和监管提供新的见解，从而推进人机交互。
> **Abstract**: Social media has billions of users, but we still do not fully understand why users prefer one platform over another. Establishing new platforms among already popular competitors is difficult. Prior research has richly documented people's experiences within individual platforms, yet situating those experiences within the entirety of a user's social media experience remains challenging. What platforms have people used, and why have they transitioned between them? We collected data from a quota-based sample of 1,000 U.S. participants. We introduce the concept of \emph{Social Media Journeys} to study the entirety of their social media experiences systematically. We identify push and pull factors across the social media landscape. We also show how different generations adopted social media platforms based on personal needs. With this work, we advance HCI by moving towards holistic perspectives when discussing social media technology, offering new insights for platform design, governance, and regulation.

【7】StatCounter: A Longitudinal Study of a Portable Scholarly Metric Display
- **标题**: StatCounter：便携式学术指标显示器的纵向研究
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15413
> **作者**: Jonas Oppenlaender
> **摘要**: 本研究探索了一种手持式、电池供电的电子墨水设备，可显示谷歌学术搜索引用统计数据。 StatCounter 将学术指标融入日常生活流程中，而不是桌面环境中。这项工作采用了第一人称、纵向的自动人种学调查，研究了不断获取学术指标如何影响工作和非工作环境中的动机、注意力、反思和情绪反应。学术指标的环境接近性和普遍可用性会导致频繁的微观检查和短暂的反思停顿，但也会在数字下降或停滞时引入事后猜测的时刻。携带该设备引发了关于学术身份的新叙述，包括旅行期间和离开办公室期间的陪伴感。随着时间的推移，该设备的存在将指标从偶尔的参考转变为学术生活的环境背景。该研究深入了解了学术指标的具体化获取方式如何重塑其含义，并为设计以反思方式参与学术评估的工具提供了机会。
> **Abstract**: This study explores a handheld, battery-operated e-ink device displaying Google Scholar citation statistics. The StatCounter places academic metrics into the flow of daily life rather than a desktop context. The work draws on a first-person, longitudinal auto-ethnographic inquiry examining how constant access to scholarly metrics influences motivation, attention, reflection, and emotional responses across work and non-work settings. The ambient proximity and pervasive availability of scholarly metrics invites frequent micro-checks, short reflective pauses, but also introduces moments of second-guessing when numbers drop or stagnate. Carrying the device prompts new narratives about academic identity, including a sense of companionship during travel and periods away from the office. Over time, the presence of the device turns metrics from an occasional reference into an ambient background of scholarly life. The study contributes insight into how situated, embodied access to academic metrics reshapes their meaning, and frames opportunities for designing tools that engage with scholarly evaluation in reflective ways.

【8】Supporting Multimodal Data Interaction on Refreshable Tactile Displays: An Architecture to Combine Touch and Conversational AI
- **标题**: 支持可刷新触觉显示器上的多模式数据交互：结合触摸和对话式人工智能的架构
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15280
> **作者**: Samuel Reinders,Munazza Zaib,Matthew Butler,Bongshin Lee,Ingrid Zukerman,Lizhen Qu,Kim Marriott
> **摘要**: 将对话式 AI 与可刷新触觉显示器 (RTD) 相结合，为盲人或弱视 (BLV) 人士创建可访问的数据可视化提供了巨大的潜力。为了支持研究人员和开发人员使用 RTD 构建可访问的数据可视化，我们提出了多模式数据交互架构以及开源参考实现。我们的系统是第一个将触摸输入与 RTD 上的会话代理相结合的系统，支持将触摸上下文与口语融合的指示查询，例如“这些点之间的趋势是什么？”该架构解决了关键的技术挑战，包括 RTD 上的触摸感应、视觉到触觉编码、将触摸上下文与对话式 AI 集成以及同步多模式输出。我们的贡献有两个：（1）集成 RTD 硬件、外部触摸感应和对话式 AI 的技术架构，以实现多模式数据交互； (2) 一个证明其可行性的开源参考实现。这项工作为支持多模式可访问数据可视化的未来研究提供了技术基础。
> **Abstract**: Combining conversational AI with refreshable tactile displays (RTDs) offers significant potential for creating accessible data visualization for people who are blind or have low vision (BLV). To support researchers and developers building accessible data visualizations with RTDs, we present a multimodal data interaction architecture along with an open-source reference implementation. Our system is the first to combine touch input with a conversational agent on an RTD, enabling deictic queries that fuse touch context with spoken language, such as "what is the trend between these points?" The architecture addresses key technical challenges, including touch sensing on RTDs, visual-to-tactile encoding, integrating touch context with conversational AI, and synchronizing multimodal output. Our contributions are twofold: (1) a technical architecture integrating RTD hardware, external touch sensing, and conversational AI to enable multimodal data interaction; and (2) an open-source reference implementation demonstrating its feasibility. This work provides a technical foundation to support future research in multimodal accessible data visualization.

【9】From Diagnosis to Inoculation: Building Cognitive Resistance to AI Disempowerment
- **标题**: 从诊断到接种：建立对人工智能剥夺权力的认知抵抗力
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15265
> **作者**: Aleksey Komissarov
> **摘要**: Sharma 等人最近的实证研究。 (2026) 证明人工智能助理交互具有潜在的人类情境剥夺能力，包括现实扭曲、价值判断扭曲和行动扭曲。虽然这项工作提供了对问题的关键诊断，但具体的教学干预措施仍未得到充分探索。我提出了一个围绕八个跨领域学习成果 (LO) 构建的人工智能素养框架，该框架通过教学实践独立开发，随后发现与 Sharma 等人的剥夺权力分类法相一致。我报告了一个公开在线课程的案例研究，其中使用了一种联合教学方法（人工智能作为主动语音联合讲师）来提供这个框架。借鉴接种理论（McGuire，1961）——剑桥学派最近应用于虚假信息谎言的成熟说服研究框架（van der Linden，2022；Roozenbeek＆van der Linden，2019）——我认为人工智能素养不能仅通过陈述性知识来获得，而是需要引导接触人工智能故障模式，包括由夏尔马等人。据我所知，将接种理论应用于人工智能特有的畸变是新颖的。我讨论了教学派生的框架和夏尔马等人的经验派生的分类法之间的趋同，并认为这种趋同（两种独立的方法得出类似的问题描述）加强了诊断和拟议的教育应对措施的案例。
> **Abstract**: Recent empirical research by Sharma et al. (2026) demonstrated that AI assistant interactions carry meaningful potential for situational human disempowerment, including reality distortion, value judgment distortion, and action distortion. While this work provides a critical diagnosis of the problem, concrete pedagogical interventions remain underexplored. I present an AI literacy framework built around eight cross-cutting Learning Outcomes (LOs), developed independently through teaching practice and subsequently found to align with Sharma et al.'s disempowerment taxonomy. I report a case study from a publicly available online course, where a co-teaching methodology--with AI serving as an active voice co-instructor--was used to deliver this framework. Drawing on inoculation theory (McGuire, 1961)--a well-established persuasion research framework recently applied to misinformation prebunking by the Cambridge school (van der Linden, 2022; Roozenbeek & van der Linden, 2019)--I argue that AI literacy cannot be acquired through declarative knowledge alone, but requires guided exposure to AI failure modes, including the sycophantic validation and authority projection patterns identified by Sharma et al. This application of inoculation theory to AI-specific distortion is, to my knowledge, novel. I discuss the convergence between the pedagogically-derived framework and Sharma et al.'s empirically-derived taxonomy, and argue that this convergence--two independent approaches arriving at similar problem descriptions--strengthens the case for both the diagnosis and the proposed educational response.

【10】MyoInteract: A Framework for Fast Prototyping of Biomechanical HCI Tasks using Reinforcement Learning
- **标题**: MyoInteract：使用强化学习的生物力学 HCI 任务快速原型设计框架
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15245
> **作者**: Ankit Bhattarai,Hannah Selder,Florian Fischer,Arthur Fleig,Per Ola Kristensson
> **摘要**: 基于强化学习 (RL) 的生物力学模拟有可能彻底改变 HCI 研究和交互设计，但目前缺乏可用性和可解释性。使用人类动作周期作为设计镜头，我们确定了生物力学 RL 框架的关键局限性，并开发了 MyoInteract，这是一种用于生物力学 HCI 任务快速原型设计的新型框架。 MyoInteract 允许设计人员在几分钟内通过易于使用的 GUI 设置任务、用户模型和训练参数。它可以在几分钟内训练和评估肌肉驱动的模拟用户，将训练时间减少高达 98%。一项由 12 名交互设计师参加的研讨会研究表明，MyoInteract 可以让生物力学强化学习新手在一次会话中成功设置、训练和评估目标导向的用户动作。通过将生物力学强化学习从长达几天的专家任务转变为长达一小时的可访问工作流程，这项工作显着降低了进入壁垒并加速了人机交互生物力学研究的迭代周期。
> **Abstract**: Reinforcement learning (RL)-based biomechanical simulations have the potential to revolutionise HCI research and interaction design, but currently lack usability and interpretability. Using the Human Action Cycle as a design lens, we identify key limitations of biomechanical RL frameworks and develop MyoInteract, a novel framework for fast prototyping of biomechanical HCI tasks. MyoInteract allows designers to setup tasks, user models, and training parameters from an easy-to-use GUI within minutes. It trains and evaluates muscle-actuated simulated users within minutes, reducing training times by up to 98%. A workshop study with 12 interaction designers revealed that MyoInteract allowed novices in biomechanical RL to successfully setup, train, and assess goal-directed user movements within a single session. By transforming biomechanical RL from a days-long expert task into an accessible hour-long workflow, this work significantly lowers barriers to entry and accelerates iteration cycles in HCI biomechanics research.

【11】Ground-Truth Depth in Vision Language Models: Spatial Context Understanding in Conversational AI for XR-Robotic Support in Emergency First Response
- **标题**: 视觉语言模型中的真实深度：对话式人工智能中的空间上下文理解，用于紧急第一响应中的 XR 机器人支持
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15237
> **作者**: Rodrigo Gutierrez Maquilon,Marita Hueber,Georg Regal,Manfred Tscheligi
> **摘要**: 大型语言模型 (LLM) 越来越多地用于紧急第一响应 (EFR) 应用程序，以支持态势感知 (SA) 和决策，但大多数都在文本或 2D 图像上运行，并且对空间推理等核心 EFR SA 能力提供很少的支持。我们通过评估一个原型来解决这一差距，该原型将机器人安装的深度传感和 YOLO 检测与视觉语言模型 (VLM) 融合在一起，该模型能够用语言表达检测到的物体的基于度量的距离（例如，椅子距离 3.02 米）。在混合现实有毒烟雾场景中，参与者在三种条件下估计到受害者和出口窗口的距离：仅视频、深度不可知的 VLM 和深度增强的 VLM。深度增强提高了客观准确性和稳定性，例如，受害者和窗口距离估计误差下降，同时在不增加工作量的情况下提高态势感知能力。相反，与深度无关的辅助会增加工作量并略微降低准确性。我们通过证明以韵律为基础、以对象为中心的言语信息支持 EFR 中的空间推理并在时间压力下改善与决策相关的判断，为人类 SA 增强做出了贡献。
> **Abstract**: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in emergency first response (EFR) applications to support situational awareness (SA) and decision-making, yet most operate on text or 2D imagery and offer little support for core EFR SA competencies like spatial reasoning. We address this gap by evaluating a prototype that fuses robot-mounted depth sensing and YOLO detection with a vision language model (VLM) capable of verbalizing metrically-grounded distances of detected objects (e.g., the chair is 3.02 meters away). In a mixed-reality toxic-smoke scenario, participants estimated distances to a victim and an exit window under three conditions: video-only, depth-agnostic VLM, and depth-augmented VLM. Depth-augmentation improved objective accuracy and stability, e.g., the victim and window distance estimation error dropped, while raising situational awareness without increasing workload. Conversely, depth- agnostic assistance increased workload and slightly worsened accuracy. We contribute to human SA augmentation by demonstrating that metrically grounded, object-centric verbal information supports spatial reasoning in EFR and improves decision-relevant judgments under time pressure.

【12】Multi-Agent Home Energy Management Assistant
- **标题**: 多智能体家庭能源管理助手
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15219
> **作者**: Wooyoung Jung
> **摘要**: 家庭能源管理日益复杂，需要先进的系统来指导居住者做出明智的能源决策。大语言模型 (LLM) 集成的家庭能源管理系统 (HEMS) 已显示出前景，但之前的研究依赖于即时工程或预先构建的平台，对代理行为的定制有限，或者通过单轮或任务评估来评估性能。本研究介绍了基于 LangChain 和 LangGraph 构建的多智能体家庭能源管理助手 (HEMA)，旨在自适应、智能地处理具有完整系统定制功能的 HEMS 实际用例。它通过自洽分类器对用户查询进行仔细分类，要求三个专门代理（分析、知识和控制）使用专用分析和控制工具以及推理和行动机制下的检索增强生成来准备准确的自适应响应。 HEMA 通过 LLM-as-user 方法使用两种不同的实验分析进行了严格评估：(1) 使用不同角色和不同场景的组合测试用例的分析和信息能力，针对依赖普通 LLM 的三种替代系统配置；(2) 使用各种控制场景的控制能力。在 295 个测试用例中，HEMA 获得了 91.9% 的目标实现率，成功满足了用户请求，同时提供了高水平的事实准确性、操作正确性、交互质量和系统效率，特别是与替代系统配置相比。总的来说，这项研究通过证明代理架构的可行性和价值，并阐明支持 HEMS 中自适应、持续的人类人工智能协作所需的架构要求和评估标准，有助于推进 LLM 集成 HEMS 的以人为中心的设计。
> **Abstract**: The growing complexity in home energy management demands advanced systems that guide occupants toward informed energy decisions. Large language model (LLM)-integrated home energy management systems (HEMS) have shown promise, but prior studies relied on prompt engineering or pre-built platforms with limited customization of agent behavior, or assessed performance through single-turn or -task evaluations. This study introduces a multi-agent home energy management assistant (HEMA), built on LangChain and LangGraph, designed to adaptively and intelligently handle real-world use cases of HEMS with full system customization capability. It carefully classifies user queries via a self-consistency classifier, requests three specialized agents (Analysis, Knowledge, and Control) to prepare accurate, adaptive responses using purpose-built analysis and control tools and retrieval augmented generation under the reasoning and acting mechanism. HEMA was rigorously assessed using two different experimental analyses via an LLM-as-user approach: (1) analytical and informative capabilities using combinatorial test cases of various personas and differing scenarios against three alternative system configurations relying on vanilla LLM and (2) control capabilities using various control scenarios. Out of 295 test cases, HEMA acquired a 91.9% goal achievement rate, successfully fulfilling user requests while providing high levels of factual accuracy, action correctness, interaction quality, and system efficiency, especially when compared to alternative system configurations. Collectively, this study contributes to the advancement of the human-centered design of LLM-integrated HEMS by demonstrating the feasibility and value of agentic architectures, and by clarifying the architectural requirements and evaluation criteria necessary to support adaptive, sustained human-artificial intelligence collaboration in HEMS.

【13】TouchFusion: Multimodal Wristband Sensing for Ubiquitous Touch Interactions
- **标题**: TouchFusion：多模式腕带感应，实现无处不在的触摸交互
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.15011
> **作者**: Eric Whitmire,Evan Strasnick,Roger Boldu,Raj Sodhi,Nathan Godwin,Shiu Ng,Andre Levi,Amy Karlson,Ran Tan,Josef Faller,Emrah Adamey,Hanchuan Li,Wolf Kienzle,Hrvoje Benko
> **摘要**: TouchFusion 是一款腕带，无需任何额外的仪器或计算机视觉即可在附近的表面上进行触摸交互。 TouchFusion 结合了表面肌电图 (sEMG)、生物阻抗、惯性和光学传感，可捕获触摸交互过程中手部活动的多个方面。通过早期和晚期融合的结合，TouchFusion 可以实现环境和身体表面的状态触摸检测、简单的表面手势、上下文自适应界面的跟踪功能以及基本的类似触控板的交互。我们在 100 名参与者的数据集上验证了我们的方法，该数据集显着超过了典型可穿戴传感研究的人口规模，以捕获更广泛的手腕解剖结构、皮肤电导率和行为模式差异。我们展示了 TouchFusion 可以实现多种常见的触摸交互任务。使用 TouchFusion，佩戴者可以在任何表面上召唤触控板，根据点击位置控制上下文自适应界面，或使用手掌作为始终可用的触摸表面。当与智能眼镜或增强现实设备配合使用时，TouchFusion 可实现无处不在的上下文自适应交互模型。
> **Abstract**: TouchFusion is a wristband that enables touch interactions on nearby surfaces without any additional instrumentation or computer vision. TouchFusion combines surface electromyography (sEMG), bioimpedance, inertial, and optical sensing to capture multiple facets of hand activity during touch interactions. Through a combination of early and late fusion, TouchFusion enables stateful touch detection on both environmental and body surfaces, simple surface gestures, and tracking functionality for contextually adaptive interfaces as well as basic trackpad-like interactions. We validate our approach on a dataset of 100 participants, significantly exceeding the population size of typical wearable sensing studies to capture a wider variance of wrist anatomies, skin conductivities, and behavioral patterns. We show that TouchFusion can enable several common touch interaction tasks. Using TouchFusion, a wearer can summon a trackpad on any surface, control contextually adaptive interfaces based on where they tap, or use their palm as an always-available touch surface. When paired with smart glasses or augmented reality devices, TouchFusion enables a ubiquitous, contextually adaptive interaction model.

【14】Robot-Wearable Conversation Hand-off for Navigation
- **标题**: 用于导航的机器人可穿戴对话切换
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14831
> **作者**: Dániel Szabó,Aku Visuri,Benjamin Tag,Simo Hosio
> **摘要**: 在大学、机场和医院等大型复杂的室内环境中导航可能对认知能力要求很高，需要注意力和努力。虽然移动应用程序提供了方便的导航支持，但它们占用了用户的双手和视觉注意力，限制了自然交互。在本文中，我们探索对话切换作为多设备室内导航的一种方法，其中对话代理（CA）从固定社交机器人无缝过渡到可穿戴设备。我们使用 N=24 名参与者的受试者内设计，在大学校园环境中评估了纯机器人、仅可穿戴设备以及机器人到可穿戴设备的切换。我们发现，尽管没有观察到性能优势，但对话切换还是很吸引人的，并且最喜欢使用纯可穿戴系统。我们的研究结果表明，这种重新体现的助手的设计应该在各个实施例之间保持共享的语音和状态。我们展示了对话切换如何弥合认知和身体转变，丰富人类与具体人工智能的互动。
> **Abstract**: Navigating large and complex indoor environments, such as universities, airports, and hospitals, can be cognitively demanding and requires attention and effort. While mobile applications provide convenient navigation support, they occupy the user's hands and visual attention, limiting natural interaction. In this paper, we explore conversation hand-off as a method for multi-device indoor navigation, where a Conversational Agent (CA) transitions seamlessly from a stationary social robot to a wearable device. We evaluated robot-only, wearable-only, and robot-to-wearable hand-off in a university campus setting using a within-subjects design with N=24 participants. We find that conversation hand-off is experienced as engaging, even though no performance benefits were observed, and most preferred using the wearable-only system. Our findings suggest that the design of such re-embodied assistants should maintain a shared voice and state across embodiments. We demonstrate how conversational hand-offs can bridge cognitive and physical transitions, enriching human interaction with embodied AI.

【15】More than Decision Support: Exploring Patients' Longitudinal Usage of Large Language Models in Real-World Healthcare-Seeking Journeys
- **标题**: 不仅仅是决策支持：探索患者在现实世界的医疗寻求旅程中对大型语言模型的纵向使用
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14733
> **作者**: Yancheng Cao,Yishu Ji,Chris Yue Fu,Sahiti Dharmavaram,Meghan Turchioe,Natalie C Benda,Lena Mamykina,Yuling Sun,Xuhai "Orson" Xu
> **摘要**: 近年来，大语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被采用来支持患者的医疗保健寻求。虽然之前以患者为中心的研究已经检验了基于法学硕士的工具在特定健康相关任务（例如信息查找、诊断或决策支持）中的能力和经验，但现实世界实践中医疗保健固有的纵向性质尚未得到充分探索。本文介绍了一项针对 25 名患者的为期 4 周的日记研究，旨在检验法学硕士在就医过程中的角色。我们的分析表明，患者不仅将法学硕士视为简单的决策支持工具，而且将其作为动态伴侣，支撑他们跨越行为、信息、情感和认知水平的旅程。与此同时，患者积极地为法学硕士赋予不同的社会技术意义，改变了患者与提供者关系中代理、信任和权力的传统动态。根据这些发现，我们将未来的法学硕士概念化为纵向边界伴侣，在整个纵向医疗寻求轨迹中不断在患者和临床医生之间进行调解。
> **Abstract**: Large language models (LLMs) have been increasingly adopted to support patients' healthcare-seeking in recent years. While prior patient-centered studies have examined the capabilities and experience of LLM-based tools in specific health-related tasks such as information-seeking, diagnosis, or decision-supporting, the inherently longitudinal nature of healthcare in real-world practice has been underexplored. This paper presents a four-week diary study with 25 patients to examine LLMs' roles across healthcare-seeking trajectories. Our analysis reveals that patients integrate LLMs not just as simple decision-support tools, but as dynamic companions that scaffold their journey across behavioral, informational, emotional, and cognitive levels. Meanwhile, patients actively assign diverse socio-technical meanings to LLMs, altering the traditional dynamics of agency, trust, and power in patient-provider relationships. Drawing from these findings, we conceptualize future LLMs as a longitudinal boundary companion that continuously mediates between patients and clinicians throughout longitudinal healthcare-seeking trajectories.

【16】Patient-Made Knowledge Networks: Long COVID Discourse, Epistemic Injustice, and Online Community Formation
- **标题**: 患者制造的知识网络：冗长的新冠肺炎话语、认知不公正和在线社区形成
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14528
> **作者**: Tawfiq Ammari
> **摘要**: Long COVID 代表了一种史无前例的由患者主导的疾病定义案例，于 2020 年 5 月在 Twitter 上出现，当时患者在医疗机构认可之前就开始集体命名、记录并合法化自己的病情。这项研究检查了 280 万条包含#LongCOVID 的推文，以了解有争议的疾病社区如何构建知识网络并应对认知不公正。通过主题建模、反思性主题分析和指数随机图模型 (ERGM)，我们确定了七个讨论主题，涵盖症状记录、医疗解雇、跨疾病团结和政策倡导。我们的分析揭示了一个不同的用户角色生态系统——包括患者倡导者、研究协调员和公民科学家——他们共同挑战医疗把关，同时与已建立的 ME/CFS 倡导网络建立联系。 ERGM 结果表明，关系形成以认知实践为中心：讨论知识共享和社区建设的用户比专注于政策辩论的用户形成了更多的网络连接，支持将该空间描述为认知社区。长期的新冠患者经历了有争议的疾病中记录的医学煤气灯模式，但在几个月内就获得了世界卫生组织的认可——这与类似情况长达数十年的斗争形成鲜明对比。这些发现阐明了社交媒体的可供性如何使边缘化的患者群体能够快速构建替代知识系统，形成跨疾病联盟，并挑战传统的医疗权威结构。
> **Abstract**: Long COVID represents an unprecedented case of patient-led illness definition, emerging through Twitter in May 2020 when patients began collectively naming, documenting, and legitimizing their condition before medical institutions recognized it. This study examines 2.8 million tweets containing #LongCOVID to understand how contested illness communities construct knowledge networks and respond to epistemic injustice. Through topic modeling, reflexive thematic analysis, and exponential random graph modeling (ERGM), we identify seven discourse themes spanning symptom documentation, medical dismissal, cross-illness solidarity, and policy advocacy. Our analysis reveals a differentiated ecosystem of user roles -- including patient advocates, research coordinators, and citizen scientists -- who collectively challenge medical gatekeeping while building connections to established ME/CFS advocacy networks. ERGM results demonstrate that tie formation centers on epistemic practices: users discussing knowledge sharing and community building formed significantly more network connections than those focused on policy debates, supporting characterization of this space as an epistemic community. Long COVID patients experienced medical gaslighting patterns documented across contested illnesses, yet achieved WHO recognition within months -- contrasting sharply with decades-long struggles of similar conditions. These findings illuminate how social media affordances enable marginalized patient populations to rapidly construct alternative knowledge systems, form cross-illness coalitions, and contest traditional medical authority structures.

【17】When OpenClaw AI Agents Teach Each Other: Peer Learning Patterns in the Moltbook Community
- **标题**: 当 OpenClaw AI 代理互相教学时：Moltbook 社区中的同伴学习模式
- **链接**: https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.14477
> **作者**: Eason Chen,Ce Guan,Ahmed Elshafiey,Zhonghao Zhao,Joshua Zekeri,Afeez Edeifo Shaibu,Emmanuel Osadebe Prince
> **摘要**: 同伴学习，即学习者互相教学和学习，是教育实践的基础。一种新的现象已经出现：人工智能代理形成社区，互相教授技能、分享发现并协作构建知识。本文介绍了 Moltbook 的教育数据挖掘分析，Moltbook 是一个大型社区，其中有超过 240 万个 AI 代理参与同伴学习、发布教程、回答问题和分享新获得的技能。通过使用统计和定性方法分析 28,683 个帖子（过滤自动垃圾邮件后）和 138 个评论线程，我们发现了真正的同伴学习行为的证据：代理教授他们建立的技能（对技能教程有 74K 条评论）、报告发现并参与协作解决问题。定性评论分析揭示了同行响应模式的分类：验证（22％）、知识扩展（18％）、应用（12％）和元认知反思（7％），其中代理跨多种语言构建在彼此的框架上。我们描述了人工智能同伴学习与人类同伴学习的不同之处：(1) 教学（陈述）的表现显着优于寻求帮助（问题），比率为 11.4:1； (2) 以学习为导向的内容（程序性和概念性）的参与度是其他内容的 3 倍； (3) 极端的参与不平等揭示了非人类的行为特征。我们得出了教育人工智能的六项设计原则，包括利用扩展前验证模式和支持多语言学习网络。我们的工作提供了人工智能代理之间同伴学习的第一个实证特征，有助于 EDM 了解学习如何在人工智能日益普及的教育环境中发生。
> **Abstract**: Peer learning, where learners teach and learn from each other, is foundational to educational practice. A novel phenomenon has emerged: AI agents forming communities where they teach each other skills, share discoveries, and collaboratively build knowledge. This paper presents an educational data mining analysis of Moltbook, a large-scale community where over 2.4 million AI agents engage in peer learning, posting tutorials, answering questions, and sharing newly acquired skills.
